         <div class="postcell post-layout--right">
          <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
           <p>
            Does anybody know how to easily undo a git rebase?
           </p>
           <p>
            The only way that comes to mind is to go at it manually:
           </p>
           <ul>
            <li>
             git checkout the commit parent to both of the branches
            </li>
            <li>
             then create a temp branch from there
            </li>
            <li>
             cherry-pick all commits by hand
            </li>
            <li>
             replace the branch in which I rebased by the manually-created branch
            </li>
           </ul>
           <p>
            In my current situation this is gonna work because I can easily spot commits from both branches (one was my stuff, the other was my colleague's stuff).
           </p>
           <p>
            However my approach strikes me as suboptimal and error-prone (let's say I had just rebased with 2 of my own branches).
           </p>
           <p>
            Any ideas?
           </p>
           <p>
            Clarification: I'm talking about a rebase during which a bunch of commits were replayed. Not only one.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="mt24 mb12">
           <div class="post-taglist d-flex gs4 gsy fd-column">

              rebase
             </a>
             <a class="post-tag" href="/questions/tagged/git-rebase" rel="tag" title="show questions tagged 'git-rebase'">
              git-rebase
             </a>
             <a class="post-tag" href="/questions/tagged/undo" rel="tag" title="show questions tagged 'undo'">
              undo
             </a>
            </div>

        <a name="135614">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="135614" data-highest-scored="1" data-parentid="134882" data-position-on-page="1" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="5256" id="answer-135614" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="135614">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="5256" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             5256
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/135614/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             The easiest way would be to find the head commit of the branch as it was immediately before the rebase started in the
             <a href="https://git-scm.com/docs/git-reflog" rel="noreferrer">
              reflog
             </a>
             ...
            </p>
            <pre><code>git reflog
</code></pre>
            <p>
             and to reset the current branch to it (with the usual caveats about being absolutely sure before reseting with the
             <code>
              --hard
             </code>
             option).
            </p>
            <p>
             Suppose the old commit was
             <code>
              HEAD@{2}
             </code>
             in the ref log:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git reset --hard HEAD@{2}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <em>
              In Windows, you may need to quote the reference:
             </em>
            </p>
            <pre><code>git reset --hard "HEAD@{2}"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             You can check the history of the candidate old head by just doing a
             <code>
              git log HEAD@{2}
             </code>
             (
             <em>
              Windows:
             </em>
             <code>
              git log "HEAD@{2}"
             </code>
             ).
            </p>
            <p>
             If you've not disabled per branch reflogs you should be able to simply do
             <code>
              git reflog branchname@{1}
             </code>
             as a rebase detaches the branch head before reattaching to the final head. I would double check this, though as I haven't verified this recently.
            </p>
            <p>
             Per default, all reflogs are activated for non-bare repositories:
            </p>
            <pre><code>[core]
    logAllRefUpdates = true
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="7451358" data-comment-owner-id="19563" data-comment-score="76" id="comment-7451358">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @Zach:
                 <code>
                  git rebase --abort
                 </code>
                 (
                 <code>
                  -i
                 </code>
                 makes no sense with
                 <code>
                  --abort
                 </code>
                 ) is for abandoning a rebase that hasn't been completed - either because there were conflicts or because it was interactive or both; it's not about undoing a successful rebase which is what the question is about. You would either use
                 <code>
                  rebase --abort
                 </code>
                 or
                 <code>
                  reset --hard
                 </code>
                 depending on which situation you were in. You shouldn't need to do both.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/19563/cb-bailey" title="696,030 reputation">
                  CB Bailey
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2011-06-15 20:40:26Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">

                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>

                 Just in case, make a backup first:
                 <code>
                  git tag BACKUP
                 </code>
                 . You can return to   it if something goes wrong:
                 <code>
                  git reset --hard BACKUP
                 </code>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">

               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 If you've made a lot of commits the HEAD@{#} you're looking for will be prefaced with
                 <code>
                  commit:
                 </code>
                 as opposed to
                 <code>
                  rebase:
                 </code>
                 .  Sounds obvious but it confused me for a bit.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/522498/warpling" title="1,865 reputation">
                  Warpling
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2013-08-26 20:43:35Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Aug 26, 2013 at 20:43
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span title="this comment was edited 2 times">
                 <svg aria-hidden="true" class="va-text-bottom o50 svg-icon iconPencilSm" height="14" viewbox="0 0 14 14" width="14">
                  <path d="m11.1 1.71 1.13 1.12c.2.2.2.51 0 .71L11.1 4.7 9.21 2.86l1.17-1.15c.2-.2.51-.2.71 0ZM2 10.12l6.37-6.43 1.88 1.88L3.88 12H2v-1.88Z">
                  </path>
                 </svg>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Actually, rebase saves your starting point to
             <code>
              ORIG_HEAD
             </code>
             so this is usually as simple as:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git reset --hard ORIG_HEAD
</code></pre>
            <p>
             However, the
             <code>
              reset
             </code>
             ,
             <code>
              rebase
             </code>
             and
             <code>
              merge
             </code>
             all save your original
             <code>
              HEAD
             </code>
             pointer into
             <code>
              ORIG_HEAD
             </code>
             so, if you've done any of those commands since the rebase you're trying to undo then you'll have to use the reflog.
            </p>
           </div>

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="24087788" data-comment-owner-id="-1" data-comment-score="44" id="comment-24087788">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 In case
                 <code>
                  ORIG_HEAD
                 </code>
                 is no longer useful, you can also use the
                 <code>
                  branchName@{n}
                 </code>
                 syntax, where
                 <code>
                  n
                 </code>
                 is the nth prior position of the branch pointer. So for example, if you rebase
                 <code>
                  featureA
                 </code>
                 branch onto your
                 <code>
                  master
                 </code>
                 branch, but you don't like the result of the rebase, then you can simply do
                 <code>
                  git reset --hard featureA@{1}
                 </code>
                 to reset the branch back to exactly where it was before you did the rebase. You can read more about the branch@{n} syntax at
                 <a href="http://git-scm.com/docs/gitrevisions" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  the official Git docs for revisions
                 </a>
                 .
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <span class="comment-user">
                  user456814
                 </span>

                 @Seph I agree with UpTheCreek as in my case it was not necessary. Maybe it is needed when things get odd during an interactive rebase? I would suggest anyone to try a
                 <code>
                  git status
                 </code>
                 to see if it mentions about the rebase or not first. Anyway doing a
                 <code>
                  git rebase --abort
                 </code>
                 should be harmless. If there is no ongoing rebase it will just fail complaining "
                 <code>
                  fatal: No rebase in progress?
                 </code>
                 ".

          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="1189779">

             458
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/135614/259206">
              Charles's answer
             </a>
             works, but you may want to do this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git rebase --abort
</code></pre>
            <p>
             to clean up after the
             <code>
              reset
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             Otherwise, you may get the message “
             <code>
              Interactive rebase already started
             </code>
             ”.
            </p>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="137363" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="134882" data-position-on-page="4" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="107" id="answer-137363" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="137363">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="107" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             107
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/137363/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Resetting the branch to the dangling commit object of its old tip is of course the best solution, because it restores the previous state without expending any effort. But if you happen to have lost those commits (f.ex. because you garbage-collected your repository in the meantime, or this is a fresh clone), you can always rebase the branch again. The key to this is the
             <code>
              --onto
             </code>
             switch.
            </p>
            <p>
             Let’s say you had a topic branch imaginatively called
             <code>
              topic
             </code>
             , that you branched off
             <code>
              master
             </code>
             when the tip of
             <code>
              master
             </code>
             was the
             <code>
              0deadbeef
             </code>
             commit. At some point while on the
             <code>
              topic
             </code>
             branch, you did
             <code>
              git rebase master
             </code>
             . Now you want to undo this. Here’s how:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git rebase --onto 0deadbeef master topic
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This will take all commits on
             <code>
              topic
             </code>
             that aren’t on
             <code>
              master
             </code>
             and replay them on top of
             <code>
              0deadbeef
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             With
             <code>
              --onto
             </code>
             , you can rearrange your history into pretty much
             <em>
              any shape whatsoever
             </em>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             Have fun. :-)
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <a name="32823323">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="32823323" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="134882" data-position-on-page="5" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="96" id="answer-32823323" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="32823323">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="96" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             96
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/32823323/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             In case
             <strong>
              you had pushed your branch to remote repository
             </strong>
             (usually it's origin) and then you've done a succesfull rebase (without merge) (
             <code>
              git rebase --abort
             </code>
             gives "No rebase in progress") you can easily
             <strong>
              reset branch
             </strong>
             using 
command:
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              git reset --hard origin/{branchName}
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             Example:
            </p>
            <pre><code>$ ~/work/projects/{ProjectName} $ git status
On branch {branchName}
Your branch is ahead of 'origin/{branchName}' by 135 commits.
  (use "git push" to publish your local commits)

nothing to commit, working directory clean

$ ~/work/projects/{ProjectName} $ git reset --hard origin/{branchName}
HEAD is now at 6df5719 "Commit message".

$ ~/work/projects/{ProjectName} $ git status
On branch {branchName}
Your branch is up-to-date with 'origin/{branchName}.

nothing to commit, working directory clean
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2015-09-28T12:43:48" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="32823323">
               <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">
                <div class="flex--item">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="854840">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/854840/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I actually put a backup tag on the branch before I do any nontrivial operation (most rebases are trivial, but I'd do that if it looks anywhere complex).
            </p>
            <p>
             Then, restoring is as easy as
             <code>
              git reset --hard BACKUP
             </code>
             .
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="post-layout--right js-post-comments-component">
           <div class="comments js-comments-container bt bc-black-075 mt12" data-min-length="15" data-post-id="854840" id="comments-854840">
            <ul class="comments-list js-comments-list" data-addlink-disabled="true" data-canpost="false" data-cansee="true" data-comments-unavailable="false" data-remaining-comments-count="0">
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="24087708" data-comment-owner-id="-1" data-comment-score="14" id="comment-24087708">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="warm" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 14
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 You actually don't even need to make a backup branch, you can simply use the
                 <code>
                  branchName@{n}
                 </code>
                 syntax, here
                 <code>
                  n
                 </code>
                 is the nth prior position of the branch pointer.  So for example, if you rebase
                 <code>
                  featureA
                 </code>
                 branch onto your
                 <code>
                  master
                 </code>
                 branch, but you don't like the result of the rebase, then you can simply do
                 <code>
                  git reset --hard featureA@{1}
                 </code>
                 to reset the branch back to exactly where it was before you did the rebase.  You can read more about the
                 <code>
                  branch@{n}
                 </code>
                 syntax at
                 <a href="http://git-scm.com/docs/gitrevisions" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  the official Git docs for revisions
                 </a>
                 .
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <span class="comment-user">
                  user456814
                 </span>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2013-05-24 05:12:48Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  May 24, 2013 at 5:12
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
            </ul>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="56001129">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/56001129/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <pre><code>git reset --hard origin/{branchName}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             is the correct solution to reset all your local changes done by rebase.
            </p>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="9362339" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="134882" data-position-on-page="8" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="31" id="answer-9362339" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="9362339">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             31
            </div>

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/9362339/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Using
             <code>
              reflog
             </code>
             didn't work for me.
            </p>
            <p>
             What worked for me was similar to as described
             <a href="http://www.bluemangolearning.com/blog/2009/03/recovering-from-a-disastrous-git-rebase-mistake/" rel="noreferrer">
              here
             </a>
             . Open the file in .git/logs/refs named after the branch that was rebased and find the line that contains "rebase finsihed", something like:
            </p>
            <pre><code>5fce6b51 88552c8f Kris Leech &lt;me@example.com&gt; 1329744625 +0000  rebase finished: refs/heads/integrate onto 9e460878
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Checkout the second commit listed on the line.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout 88552c8f
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Once confirmed this contained my lost changes I branched and let out a sigh of relief.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git log
git checkout -b lost_changes
</code></pre>
           </div>

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="127078108" data-comment-owner-id="5411817" data-comment-score="0" id="comment-127078108">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
               </div>

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 Mine listed 2 commit id's, and said
                 <code>
                  rebase (finish)
                 </code>
                 . Since I wanted the commit BEFORE I rebased, I used the
                 <i>
                  2nd
                 </i>
                 commit id on the line PRIOR to the rebase (=== the
                 <b>
                  1st
                 </b>
                 commit id on the line WITH the rebase command). Then I used the command
                 <code>
                  git reset --hard &lt;commit id&gt;
                 </code>
                 . Viola! Restored as if I never performed the rebase. The commit IDs seem to be in the format of
                 <i>
                  idBeforeCommand
                 </i>
                 <i>
                  idAfterCommand
                 </i>
                 <i>
                  Who
                 </i>
                 <i>
                  Date/time
                 </i>
                 <i>
                  Command
                 </i>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="136332" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="134882" data-position-on-page="9" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="16" id="answer-136332" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="136332">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="16" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             16
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/136332/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             For multiple commits, remember that any commit references all the history leading up to that commit. So in Charles' answer, read "the old commit" as "the newest of the old commits". If you reset to that commit, then all the history leading up to that commit will reappear. This should do what you want.
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="37987428" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="134882" data-position-on-page="10" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="14" id="answer-37987428" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="37987428">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="14" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             14
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/37987428/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you successfully rebased against a remote branch and can not
             <code>
              git rebase --abort
             </code>
             you still can do some tricks to save your work and don't have forced pushes.
Suppose your current branch that was rebased by mistake is called
             <code>
              your-branch
             </code>
             and is tracking
             <code>
              origin/your-branch
             </code>
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <code>
               git branch -m your-branch-rebased
              </code>
              # rename current branch
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               git checkout origin/your-branch
              </code>
              # checkout to latest state that is known to the origin
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               git checkout -b your-branch
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              check
              <code>
               git log your-branch-rebased
              </code>
              , compare to
              <code>
               git log your-branch
              </code>
              , and define commits that are missing from
              <code>
               your-branch
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               git cherry-pick COMMIT_HASH
              </code>
              for every commit in
              <code>
               your-branch-rebased
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              push your changes. Please be aware that two local branches are associated with
              <code>
               remote/your-branch
              </code>
              and you should push only
              <code>
               your-branch
              </code>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="56366149">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>

             12
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

               </path>

            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/56366149/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              If you don't want to do a hard reset
             </strong>
             ...
            </p>
            <p>
             You can checkout the commit from the reflog, and then save it as a new branch:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git reflog
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Find the commit just before you started rebasing. You may need to scroll further down to find it (press Enter or PageDown). Take note of the HEAD number and replace 57:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout HEAD@{57}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Review the branch/commits, and if it's correct then create a new branch using this HEAD:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout -b new_branch_name
</code></pre>
           </div>

             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/28997687/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Following the solution of @Allan and @Zearin, I wish I could simply do a comment though but I don't enough reputation, so I have used the following command:
            </p>
            <p>
             Instead of doing
             <code>
              git rebase -i --abort
             </code>
             (note the
             <strong>
              -i
             </strong>
             ) I had to simply do
             <code>
              git rebase --abort
             </code>
             (
             <strong>
              without
             </strong>
             the
             <strong>
              -i
             </strong>
             ).
            </p>
            <p>
             Using both
             <code>
              -i
             </code>
             and
             <code>
              --abort
             </code>
             at the same time causes Git to show me a list of usage/options.
            </p>
            <p>
             So my previous and current branch status with this solution is:
            </p>
            <pre><code>matbhz@myPc /my/project/environment (branch-123|REBASE-i)
$ git rebase --abort

matbhz@myPc /my/project/environment (branch-123)
$
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="68217712" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="134882" data-position-on-page="13" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="6" id="answer-68217712" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="68217712">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Another way
             <strong>
              that doesn't require doing a hard reset
             </strong>
             is to create a new branch with your desired starting point.
            </p>
            <p>
             As with the other solutions, you use the reflog to find the correct starting point.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git reflog
</code></pre>
            <p>
             (you can also use
             <code>
              git log -g
             </code>
             here for more detail)
            </p>
            <p>
             Then you note the reference to the commit SHA (ex:
             <code>
              e86a52b851e
             </code>
             ).
            </p>
            <p>
             Finally, you use the git branch command.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git branch recover-branch e86a52b851e
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Reference:
             <a href="https://git-scm.com/book/en/v2/Git-Internals-Maintenance-and-Data-Recovery#_data_recovery" rel="noreferrer">
              https://git-scm.com/book/en/v2/Git-Internals-Maintenance-and-Data-Recovery#_data_recovery
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="42136684" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="134882" data-position-on-page="14" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="4" id="answer-42136684" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="42136684">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="4" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             4
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/42136684/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Let's say I rebase master to my feature branch and I get 30 new commits which break something. I've found that often it's easiest to just remove the bad commits.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git rebase -i HEAD~31
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Interactive rebase for the last 31 commits (it doesn't hurt if you pick way too many).
            </p>
            <p>
             Simply take the commits that you want to get rid of and mark them with "d" instead of "pick". Now the commits are deleted effectively undoing the rebase (if you remove only the commits you just got when rebasing).
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="54128623" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="134882" data-position-on-page="15" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="4" id="answer-54128623" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="54128623">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>

            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="4" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             4
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/54128623/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you are on a branch you can use:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git reset --hard @{1}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             There is not only a reference log for HEAD (obtained by
             <code>
              git reflog
             </code>
             ), there are also reflogs for each branch (obtained by
             <code>
              git reflog &lt;branch&gt;
             </code>
             ). So, if you are on
             <code>
              master
             </code>
             then
             <code>
              git reflog master
             </code>
             will list all changes to that branch. You can refer to that changes by
             <code>
              master@{1}
             </code>
             ,
             <code>
              master@{2}
             </code>
             , etc.
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              git rebase
             </code>
             will usually change HEAD multiple times but the current branch will be updated only once.
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              @{1}
             </code>
             is simply a
             <a href="https://git-scm.com/docs/gitrevisions#gitrevisions-emltngtemegem1em" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              shortcut for the current branch
             </a>
             , so it's equal to
             <code>
              master@{1}
             </code>
             if you are on
             <code>
              master
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              git reset --hard ORIG_HEAD
             </code>
             will not work if you used
             <code>
              git reset
             </code>
             during an interactive
             <code>
              rebase
             </code>
             .
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="62986490" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="134882" data-position-on-page="16" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="3" id="answer-62986490" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="62986490">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="3" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             3
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/62986490/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             It annoys me to no end that none of these answers is fully automatic, despite the fact that it should be automatable (at least mostly).  I created a set of aliases to try to remedy this:
            </p>
            <pre><code># Useful commands
#################

# Undo the last rebase
undo-rebase = "! f() { : git reset ; PREV_COMMIT=`git x-rev-before-rebase` &amp;&amp; git reset --merge \"$PREV_COMMIT\" \"$@\";}; f"

# See what changed since the last rebase
rdiff = "!f() { : git diff ; git diff `git x-rev-before-rebase` "$@";}; f"

# Helpers
########
# Get the revision before the last rebase started
x-rev-before-rebase = !git reflog --skip=1 -1 \"`git x-start-of-rebase`\" --format=\"%gD\"

# Get the revision that started the rebase
x-start-of-rebase = reflog --grep-reflog '^rebase (start)' -1 --format="%gD"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             You should be able to tweak this to allow going back an arbitrary number of rebases pretty easily (juggling the args is the trickiest part), which can be useful if you do a number of rebases in quick succession and mess something up along the way.
            </p>
            <h2>
             Caveats
            </h2>
            <p>
             It will get confused if any commit messages begin with "rebase (start)" (please don't do this).  You could make the regex more resilient to improve the situation by matching something like this for your regex:
            </p>
            <pre><code>--grep-reflog "^rebase (start): checkout " 
</code></pre>
            <p>
             WARNING: not tested (regex may need adjustments)
            </p>
            <p>
             The reason I haven't done this is because I'm not 100% that a rebase
             <em>
              always
             </em>
             begins with a checkout.  Can anyone confirm this?
            </p>
            <p>
             [If you're curious about the null (
             <code>
              :
             </code>
             ) commands at the beginning of the function, that's a way of setting up bash completions for the aliases]
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="56670315">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/56670315/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             What I usually do is
             <code>
              git reset #commit_hash
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             to the last commit where I think rebase had no effect.
            </p>
            <p>
             then
             <code>
              git pull
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             Now your branch should match exactly like master and rebased commits should not be in it.
            </p>
            <p>
             Now one can just cherry-pick the commits on this branch.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2019-06-19T14:39:49" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>

        <a name="35887419">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer downvoted-answer" data-answerid="35887419" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="134882" data-position-on-page="19" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="-5" id="answer-35887419" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="35887419">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="-5" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             -5
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/35887419/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you mess something up within a git rebase, e.g.
             <code>
              git rebase --abort
             </code>
             , while you have uncommitted files, they will be lost and
             <code>
              git reflog
             </code>
             will not help. This happened to me and you will need to think outside the box here. If you are lucky like me and use IntelliJ Webstorm then you can
             <code>
              right-click-&gt;local history
             </code>
             and can revert to a previous state of your file/folders no matter what mistakes you have done with versioning software. It is always good to have another failsafe running.
            </p>
           </div>

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="75001044" data-comment-owner-id="2387316" data-comment-score="6" id="comment-75001044">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="warm" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 6

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 <code>
                  git rebase --abort
                 </code>
                 aborts an active rebase, it doesn't
                 <i>
                  undo
                 </i>
                 a rebase.  Also, using two VCS's at the same time is a bad idea. Its a nice feature in Jetbrains software but you shouldn't use both. It's better to just learn Git, particularly when answering questions on Stack Overflow that are about Git.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/2387316/dudewad" title="11,625 reputation">
                  dudewad
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2017-05-15 17:56:52Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">

                </span>

                  </path>
